In the hour of trial, Je-sus, plead for me; Lest by base de - ni - al I de-part from Thee;\n2 HOH\nHIGH\n288\n2\n\353\217\231\353\252\205 \353\217\231\355\226\211 1\354\235\274 \354\236\204\353\252\205 8101\353\217\231 \353\217\231\353\252\205 \354\230\201 1\353\223\261 1\354\235\274\na\n0\nWhen Thou see\'st me wav-er, With a look re - call, Nor for fear or fa - vor\nP-R\no 12 a\ne do e\n96\n200\nIn the Hour of Trial.\n1 In the hour of trial,\nJesus, plead for me;\nLest by base denial\nI depart from Thee;\nWhen Thou see\'st me waver,\nWith a look recall,\nNor for fear or favor\nSuffer me to fall.\nSpread to work me harm;\nBring to my remembrance\n2 With forbidden pleasures\nWould this vain world charm;\nOr its sordid treasures\nSad Gethsemane,\nOr, in darker semblance,\nCross-crown\'d Calvary.\nH2H\n3 Should Thy merey send me\nSorrow, toil; and woe;\nOr should pain attend me\nOn my path below;\nGrant that I may never\nFail Thy hand to see;\nGrant that I may ever\nCast my care on Thee.\nHSH\nHett\n(38)\nE. G. MONK (1819-).\ndodf\na\n0-6\nSuf-fer me to\n4 When my last hour cometh,\nFraught with strife and pain,\nWhen my dust returneth\nTo the dust again;\nOn Thy truth relying,\nThrough that mortal strife,\nJesus, take me, dying,\nTo eternal life.\nHPH\nfall.\nH2H\nJames Montgomery (1771-1854).\n93\n2 Cor. xii: 9. (TUNE VIRGO.)\n1 Let me but hear my Saviour say,\n\"Strength shall be equal to thy day;\"\nThen I rejoice in deep distress,\nLeaning on all-sufficient grace.\n2 I can do all things or can bear\nAll suffering, if my Lord be there;\nSweet pleasures mingle with the pains,\nWhile He my sinking head sustains.\n3 I glory in infirmity,\nThat Christ\'s own power may rest on me;\nWhen I am weak, then am I strong;\nGrace is my shield, and Christ my song.\nRev. Isaac Watts (1674-1748)."
